Block shots to mark camera, lighting and cast positions for the shoot.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"tools-tier\">\n\t\t\t\t<img src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/celtx.com/production/www/cx-static/5.45/assets/5.45/images/tool1-3.png\">\n\t\t\t\t<h3>Prepare to save</h3>\n\t\t\t\t<p>Breakdown the script to make sure all talent, props, wardrobe, equipment, locations and crew are ready and waiting for the shoot.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"tools-tier\">\n\t\t\t\t<img src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/celtx.com/production/www/cx-static/5.45/assets/5.45/images/tool2-1.png\">\n\t\t\t\t<h3>Ready. aim. shoot.</h3>\n\t\t\t\t<p>Create a list of every shot for production.
